name: sist-hab
services:
  dbsh:
    command:
      - --default-authentication-plugin=mysql_native_password
      - --wait_timeout=28800
      - --interactive_timeout=28800
      - --max_allowed_packet=256M
      - --log-error-verbosity=2
      - --bind-address=0.0.0.0
    container_name: sist-hab-db-prod
    environment:
      MYSQL_DATABASE: sisthabpro
      MYSQL_PASSWORD: quanium
      MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD: quanium
      MYSQL_USER: quanium
      TZ: America/Bogota
    healthcheck:
      test:
        - CMD-SHELL
        - mysqladmin ping -h localhost -u root -pquanium || exit 1
      timeout: 10s
      interval: 10s
      retries: 20
      start_period: 2m0s
    image: mysql:8.1.0
    networks:
      app-network: null
    ports:
      - mode: ingress
        target: 3306
        published: "3306"
        protocol: tcp
    restart: always

      - type: volume
        source: mysql_data
        target: /var/lib/mysql
        volume: {}

        source: /home/server/sistema-habilitador/db/sisthabpro.sql

          create_host_path: true
